SOV_media_leaning_calculate_XY = {
	SOV = {
		clamp_variable = { var = SOV_media_leans_eastern_conservative min = 0 }		#Clamp / correct the variables
		clamp_variable = { var = SOV_media_leans_eastern_liberal min = 0 }
		clamp_variable = { var = SOV_media_leans_ultranationalist min = 0 }
	
		set_temp_variable = { sum = SOV_media_leans_eastern_conservative }
		add_to_temp_variable  = { sum = SOV_media_leans_eastern_liberal }
		add_to_temp_variable  = { sum = SOV_media_leans_ultranationalist }
		
		multiply_variable = { SOV_media_leans_eastern_conservative = 100 }
		divide_variable = { SOV_media_leans_eastern_conservative = sum }
		multiply_variable = { SOV_media_leans_eastern_liberal = 100 }
		divide_variable = { SOV_media_leans_eastern_liberal = sum }
		multiply_variable = { SOV_media_leans_ultranationalist = 100 }
		divide_variable = { SOV_media_leans_ultranationalist = sum }
	
		set_variable = { SOV_media_dot_Y = -100 }
		subtract_from_variable = { SOV_media_dot_Y = SOV_media_leans_eastern_liberal }
		subtract_from_variable = { SOV_media_dot_Y = SOV_media_leans_ultranationalist }
		add_to_variable = { SOV_media_dot_Y = SOV_media_leans_eastern_conservative }
		multiply_variable = { SOV_media_dot_Y = -1.78 }
		
		set_variable = { SOV_media_dot_X = SOV_media_leans_eastern_liberal }
		subtract_from_variable = { SOV_media_dot_X = SOV_media_leans_ultranationalist }
		multiply_variable = { SOV_media_dot_X = 2.03 }
		
		add_to_variable = { SOV_media_dot_Y = 11 }
		add_to_variable = { SOV_media_dot_X = 239 }
		
		set_variable = { eastern_conservative_drift_from_media = SOV_media_leans_eastern_conservative }
		divide_variable = { eastern_conservative_drift_from_media = 250 }
		set_variable = { eastern_liberal_drift_from_media = SOV_media_leans_eastern_liberal }
		divide_variable = { eastern_liberal_drift_from_media = 250 }
		set_variable = { ultranationalist_drift_from_media = SOV_media_leans_ultranationalist }
		divide_variable = { ultranationalist_drift_from_media = 250 }

		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = SOV_media_information_warfare_enabled }

			#Putinism - political shit
			set_variable = { SOV_media_pp_gain = SOV_media_leans_eastern_conservative }
			divide_variable = { SOV_media_pp_gain = 100 }
			divide_variable = { SOV_media_pp_gain = 5 }

			set_variable = { SOV_media_stability_factor = SOV_media_leans_eastern_conservative }
			divide_variable = { SOV_media_stability_factor = 1100 }

			#Nationalism - war support and army buffs

			set_variable = { SOV_media_morale_factor = SOV_media_leans_ultranationalist }
			divide_variable = { SOV_media_morale_factor = 600 }

			set_variable = { SOV_media_war_support_casualties = SOV_media_leans_ultranationalist }
			divide_variable = { SOV_media_war_support_casualties = 10000 }

			#Westernization - trade opinion and advisor cost

			set_variable = { SOV_media_trade_factor = SOV_media_leans_eastern_liberal }
			divide_variable = { SOV_media_trade_factor = 150 }

			set_variable = { SOV_media_advisor_cost_factor = SOV_media_leans_eastern_liberal }
			divide_variable = { SOV_media_advisor_cost_factor = -160 }
		}
	}
}

SOV_propaganda_event_effect={
	add_popularity = { ideology = eastern_conservative popularity = 0.002 }
}

increase_eastern_conservative_programming_by_1={
	add_to_variable = { SOV_media_leans_eastern_conservative = 1 }
	subtract_from_variable = { SOV_media_leans_eastern_liberal = 0.5 }
	subtract_from_variable = { SOV_media_leans_ultranationalist = 0.5 }
	custom_effect_tooltip = increase_eastern_conservative_programming_by_1_tt
	SOV_media_leaning_calculate_XY = yes
}
increase_eastern_conservative_programming_by_2={
	add_to_variable = { SOV_media_leans_eastern_conservative = 2 }
	subtract_from_variable = { SOV_media_leans_eastern_liberal = 1 }
	subtract_from_variable = { SOV_media_leans_ultranationalist = 1 }
	custom_effect_tooltip = increase_eastern_conservative_programming_by_2_tt
	SOV_media_leaning_calculate_XY = yes
}

SOV_clamp_influences = {
	SOV = {
		clamp_variable = { var = liberal_faction_strength min = 0 }		#Clamp / correct the variables
		clamp_variable = { var = technocrat_faction_strength min = 0 }
		clamp_variable = { var = oil_and_gas_faction_strength min = 0 }
		clamp_variable = { var = siloviki_faction_strength min = 0 }
		clamp_variable = { var = putinist_faction_strength min = 0 }
		clamp_variable = { var = nationalist_faction_strength min = 0 }
	
		set_temp_variable = { sum = liberal_faction_strength }
		add_to_temp_variable  = { sum = technocrat_faction_strength }
		add_to_temp_variable  = { sum = oil_and_gas_faction_strength }
		add_to_temp_variable  = { sum = siloviki_faction_strength }
		add_to_temp_variable  = { sum = putinist_faction_strength }
		add_to_temp_variable  = { sum = nationalist_faction_strength }
		
		multiply_variable = { liberal_faction_strength = 100 }
		divide_variable = { liberal_faction_strength = sum }
		multiply_variable = { technocrat_faction_strength = 100 }
		divide_variable = { technocrat_faction_strength = sum }
		multiply_variable = { oil_and_gas_faction_strength = 100 }
		divide_variable = { oil_and_gas_faction_strength = sum }
		multiply_variable = { siloviki_faction_strength = 100 }
		divide_variable = { siloviki_faction_strength = sum }
		multiply_variable = { putinist_faction_strength = 100 }
		divide_variable = { putinist_faction_strength = sum }
		multiply_variable = { nationalist_faction_strength = 100 }
		divide_variable = { nationalist_faction_strength = sum }
	}
}

SOV_increase_liberal_faction_small={
	custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_increase_liberal_faction_small_tt
	add_to_variable = { liberal_faction_strength = 1 }
	subtract_from_variable  = { technocrat_faction_strength = 0.2 }
	subtract_from_variable  = { oil_and_gas_faction_strength = 0.2 }
	subtract_from_variable  = { siloviki_faction_strength = 0.2 }
	subtract_from_variable  = { putinist_faction_strength = 0.2 }
	subtract_from_variable  = { nationalist_faction_strength = 0.2 }

get_faction_positions={
	clear_slot_flags = yes
	get_next_available_liberal_slot = yes
	get_next_available_technocrat_slot = yes
	get_next_available_oil_and_gas_slot = yes
	get_next_available_siloviki_slot = yes
	get_next_available_putinist_slot = yes
	get_next_available_nationalist_slot = yes

	if={							#NAVALNY
		limit={
			has_country_flag = alexei_navalny_liberal_leader_flag
			NOT = { has_country_flag = alexei_navalny_not_active_flag }
			check_variable = { var = SOV_alexei_navalny_faction value = 1 compare = equals }
		}
		set_variable = { SOV.alexei_navalny_X = 85 }
		set_variable = { SOV.alexei_navalny_Y = 181 }
	}
	else_if={
		limit={
			NOT = { has_country_flag = alexei_navalny_liberal_leader_flag }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = alexei_navalny_not_active_flag }
			check_variable = { var = SOV_alexei_navalny_faction value = 1 compare = equals }
		}
		set_variable = { SOV.alexei_navalny_X = next_available_liberal_X }
		set_variable = { SOV.alexei_navalny_Y = next_available_liberal_Y }
		get_next_available_liberal_slot = yes
	}
	else_if={
		limit={
			has_country_flag = alexei_navalny_technocrat_leader_flag

			NOT = { has_country_flag = denis_manturov_not_active_flag }
			check_variable = { var = SOV_denis_manturov_faction value = 6 compare = equals }
		}
		set_variable = { SOV.denis_manturov_X = 1055 }
		set_variable = { SOV.denis_manturov_Y = 181 }
	}
	else_if={
		limit={
			NOT = { has_country_flag = denis_manturov_nationalist_leader_flag }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = denis_manturov_not_active_flag }
			check_variable = { var = SOV_denis_manturov_faction value = 6 compare = equals }
		}
		set_variable = { SOV.denis_manturov_X = next_available_nationalist_X }
		set_variable = { SOV.denis_manturov_Y = next_available_nationalist_Y }
		get_next_available_nationalist_slot = yes
	}
}

		limit={ check_variable = { var = SOV_nikolai_patrushev_faction value = 5 compare = equals } }
		SOV_increase_putinist_faction_large = yes
	}
	else_if={
		limit={ check_variable = { var = SOV_nikolai_patrushev_faction value = 6 compare = equals } }
		SOV_increase_nationalist_faction_large = yes
	}
	
	if={
		limit = {
			has_any_power_balance = yes
			has_country_flag = putin_siloviki_power_balance
		}
		add_power_balance_value = {
			id = SOV_power_balance
			value = -0.2
		}
	}
}
get_patrushev_fire_effect={
	if={
		limit={ check_variable = { var = SOV_nikolai_patrushev_faction value = 1 compare = equals } }
		SOV_decrease_liberal_faction_large = yes
	}
	else_if={
		limit={ check_variable = { var = SOV_nikolai_patrushev_faction value = 2 compare = equals } }
		SOV_decrease_technocrat_faction_large = yes
	}
	else_if={
		limit={ check_variable = { var = SOV_nikolai_patrushev_faction value = 3 compare = equals } }
		SOV_decrease_oil_and_gas_faction_large = yes
	}
	else_if={
		limit={ check_variable = { var = SOV_nikolai_patrushev_faction value = 4 compare = equals } }
		SOV_decrease_siloviki_faction_large = yes
	}
	else_if={
		limit={ check_variable = { var = SOV_nikolai_patrushev_faction value = 5 compare = equals } }
		SOV_decrease_putinist_faction_large = yes
	}
	else_if={
		limit={ check_variable = { var = SOV_nikolai_patrushev_faction value = 6 compare = equals } }
		SOV_decrease_nationalist_faction_large = yes
	}
	
	if={
		limit = {
			has_any_power_balance = yes
			has_country_flag = putin_siloviki_power_balance
		}
		add_power_balance_value = {
			id = SOV_power_balance
			value = 0.2
		}
	}
}

SOV_load_KRP_mutiny={
	hidden_effect = { 
		news_event = { id = atd_news.63 hours = 2 } 
		
		create_dynamic_country = {
			original_tag = SOV

			spawn_new_country_economy = yes
			set_variable = { THIS.inflation_rate = SOV.inflation_rate }

			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = fascist
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = fascist
				popularity = 1
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = KRP
			set_research_slots = 4

			set_party_name = { ideology = fascist long_name = club_of_angry_patriots_subideology_party_long name = club_of_angry_patriots_subideology_party }
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Igor Girkin"
				picture = gfx/leaders/DON/Portrait_Igor_Girkin.png
				ideology = club_of_angry_patriots_subideology
				traits = { SOV_war_hero }
			}

			add_ideas = {
				limited_conscription
				authoritarian_democracy
				war_economy
				state_controlled_press
				bipolarist
				womens_rights_traditional_values
				lgbtq_rights_banned
				minority_rights_societal_discrimination
				religion_law_religious
				nationalism_laws_jingoistic
			}

			transfer_state = 430
			transfer_state = 25
			transfer_state = 88
			
			every_state={
				limit = {
					is_core_of = UKR
					NOT = { is_owned_by = SOV }
					is_fully_controlled_by = SOV
				}
				
				set_state_controller_to = KRP
			}

#				every_state={
#					limit={ is_controlled_by = KRP }
#					teleport_armies = {
#						limit = { NOT = { tag = KRP } }
#						to_state_array = owned_controlled_states
#					}
#				}

			declare_war_on = {
				target = UKR
				type = take_state_focus
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = SOV
				type = civil_war
			}

			add_civil_war_target = SOV
		}
		
		SOV = {
			transfer_units_fraction = {
				target = KRP
				size = 0.2
				stockpile_ratio = 0.1
				army_ratio = 0.2
				navy_ratio = 0.1
				air_ratio = 0.1

				keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							is_character = SOV_sergey_shoygu 
							is_character = SOV_sergey_shoygu_rework 

							is_character = SOV_valery_gerasimov_rework 
							is_character = SOV_valery_gerasimov
							
							is_character = SOV_alexander_bortnikov_rework 
							is_character = SOV_alexander_bortnikov
						}
					}

				}
			}
		}
		
		KRP = { change_tag_from  = SOV }
		KRP = { country_event = { id = russia.1101 hours = 8 } }
	}
}

SMO_load_SMA_leader={
	BLR={ puppet = SMA end_puppet = SMA faction_leader  = { remove_from_faction = SMA } }
	
	SMA={
		kill_country_leader = yes
		
		meta_effect = {
			text = {
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "[COUNTRY_LEADER_NAME]"
					picture = gfx/leaders/OTHER/Portrait_Kupalinka.png
					ideology = [COUNTRY_LEADER_IDEOLOGY_GROUP]
					traits = {  }
				}
			}
			COUNTRY_LEADER_NAME = "[BLR.GetLeader]"
			COUNTRY_LEADER_IDEOLOGY_GROUP = "[?BLR.country_leader.GetIdeologyGroup]"
		}
		
		if={
			limit = { has_war = yes }
			every_enemy_country={
				white_peace = PREV
			}
		}
	}
}

SOV_close_western_front_effect={
	clr_global_flag = smo_western_front_open
	if={
		limit = { 
			BLR = { exists = yes OR = { is_puppet_of = SOV is_in_faction_with = SOV } } 
			NOT = { 435 = { is_core_of = SOV } }
		}
		SMA={		
			transfer_state = 435
			add_state_core  = 435
			
			SMO_load_SMA_leader = yes
			
			give_military_access = SOV
			SOV = { give_military_access = SMA }
			give_military_access = BLR
			BLR = { give_military_access = SMA }
		}
	}
	else_if={
		limit = { 
			NOT={
				any_state = { OCCUPATION_is_belarus_trigger = yes is_owned_by = BLR }
			}
			435 = { is_owned_by = SOV }
		}
		SMB={
			transfer_state = 435
			add_state_core  = 435
			
			SMO_load_SMB_leader = yes
			
			give_military_access = SOV
			SOV = { give_military_access = SMB }
			
		}
	}
}

			NOT = { 434 = { is_core_of = SOV } }
		}
		SMA={
			transfer_state = 434
			add_state_core  = 434
			
			SMO_load_SMA_leader = yes

			give_military_access = SOV
			SOV = { give_military_access = SMA }
			give_military_access = BLR
			BLR = { give_military_access = SMA }
		}
	}
	else_if={
		limit = { 
			NOT={
				any_state = { OCCUPATION_is_belarus_trigger = yes is_owned_by = BLR }
			}
			434 = { is_owned_by = SOV }
		}
		SMB={
			transfer_state = 434
			add_state_core  = 434
			
			SMO_load_SMB_leader = yes
			
			give_military_access = SOV
			SOV = { give_military_access = SMB }
		}
	}
	
	SMB={
		SMO_load_SMB_leader = yes
		
		transfer_state = 446
		transfer_state = 447
		transfer_state = 448
		add_state_core = 446
		add_state_core = 447
		add_state_core = 448
		
		give_military_access = SOV
		SOV = { give_military_access = SMB }
	}

	UKR = {
		every_state={
            limit={
                OR = {
					state = 55
					state = 56
					state = 54
					state = 53
					state = 63
					state = 70
					state = 82

					state = 39
					state = 50
					state = 66

					state = 446
					state = 447
					state = 448
				}
            }
            teleport_armies = {
                limit = {
                    tag = UKR
                }
                to_state = 70
            }
        }
	}
	SOV = {
		every_state={
            limit={
                OR = {
					state = 55
					state = 56
					state = 54
					state = 53
					state = 63
					state = 70
					state = 82

					state = 39
					state = 50
					state = 66

					state = 446
					state = 447
					state = 448
				}
            }
            teleport_armies = {
                limit = {
                    tag = SOV
                }
                to_state = 50
            }
        }
	}
	UKR = {
		transfer_state = 55
		transfer_state = 56
		transfer_state = 54
		transfer_state = 53
		transfer_state = 63
		transfer_state = 70
		transfer_state = 82
	}
	SOV = {

}

SOV_open_western_front_effect={
	set_global_flag = smo_western_front_open
	if={
		limit={ SMA={ owns_state = 435 } }
		SMA={remove_state_core = 435 }
		SOV={ transfer_state = 435 add_state_claim = 435 }
	}
	else_if={
		limit={ SMB={ owns_state = 435 } }
		SMB={remove_state_core = 435 }
		SOV={ transfer_state = 435 add_state_claim = 435 }
	}
}

SOV_increase_nadezhdin_signatures = {
	custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_stopping_boris_nadezhdin_add_signatures_tt
	hidden_effect={
		add_to_variable = { SOV_boris_nadazhdin_signatures = SOV_boris_nadazhdin_signatures_weekly_gain }
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = neoliberal
			popularity = 0.015
		}
		if = {
			limit = { OR = { check_variable = { SOV_boris_nadazhdin_signatures > 105000 } check_variable = { SOV_boris_nadazhdin_signatures = 105000 } } }
	
			clr_country_flag = SOV_stopping_boris_nadezhdin_enabled
			country_event = { id = russia.1143 days = 2 }	
		}
	}

}

SOV_decrease_300_nadezhdin_signatures_weekly = {
	custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_decrease_300_nadezhdin_signatures_weekly
	hidden_effect={
		add_to_variable = { SOV_boris_nadazhdin_signatures_weekly_gain = -300 }
	}
}
